						name = "Kronshtadt Class"
						type = carrier_3
						allow_without_tech = yes
						upgrades = {
							ship_deckspace_upgrade = 3
							carrier_armor_upgrade = 3
							ship_engine_upgrade = 3
							ship_reliability_upgrade = 2
						}
					}
					create_equipment_variant = {
						name = "Okean Class"
						type = carrier_1
						allow_without_tech = yes
						upgrades = {
							ship_deckspace_upgrade = 0
							carrier_armor_upgrade = 0
							ship_engine_upgrade = 1
							ship_reliability_upgrade = 1
						}
					}
					add_equipment_production = {
						equipment = {
							type = carrier_3
							creator = "RUS"
							version_name = "Kronshtadt Class"
						}
						requested_factories = 1
						progress = 0.25
						amount = 1
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_tech = basic_carrier }
					create_equipment_variant = {
						name = "Kronshtadt Class"
						type = carrier_2
						allow_without_tech = yes
						upgrades = {
							ship_deckspace_upgrade = 2
							carrier_armor_upgrade = 2
							ship_engine_upgrade = 2
							ship_reliability_upgrade = 2
						}
					}
					create_equipment_variant = {
						name = "Okean Class"
						type = carrier_1
						allow_without_tech = yes
						upgrades = {
							ship_deckspace_upgrade = 0
							carrier_armor_upgrade = 0
							ship_engine_upgrade = 1
							ship_reliability_upgrade = 1
						}
					}
					add_equipment_production = {
						equipment = {
							type = carrier_2
							creator = "RUS"
							version_name = "Kronshtadt Class"
						}
						requested_factories = 1
						progress = 0.25
						amount = 1
					}
				}
				else = { #Carrier 1
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { has_tech = early_carrier } }
						set_technology = { early_carrier = 1 }
					}
					create_equipment_variant = {
						name = "Kronshtadt Class"
						type = carrier_1
						allow_without_tech = yes
						upgrades = {
							ship_deckspace_upgrade = 2
							carrier_armor_upgrade = 1
							ship_engine_upgrade = 2
							ship_reliability_upgrade = 1
						}
					}
					create_equipment_variant = {
						name = "Okean Class"
						type = carrier_1
						allow_without_tech = yes
						upgrades = {
							ship_deckspace_upgrade = 0
							carrier_armor_upgrade = 0
							ship_engine_upgrade = 1
							ship_reliability_upgrade = 1
						}
					}
					add_equipment_production = {
						equipment = {
							type = carrier_1
							creator = "RUS"
							version_name = "Kronshtadt Class"
						}
						requested_factories = 1
						progress = 0.25
						amount = 1
					}
				}
			}
		}
